CREATE TABLE case (case_id INT PRIMARY KEY, case_name STRING, lawyer_id INT, client_id INT, FOREIGN KEY (lawyer_id) REFERENCES lawyer(id), FOREIGN KEY (client_id) REFERENCES client(id))
